Page: 34, Font Size: 12.0, Upper: False, Bold: True, block number: 1, Text: Reconciliations to GAAP Financial Measures
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 2, Text: (Dollars in millions, except per share information)
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: The Corporation evaluates its business based on the following ratios that utilize tangible equity, a non-GAAP financial measure. Tangible equity represents shareholders' equity or 
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: common shareholders' equity reduced by goodwill and intangible assets (excluding mortgage servicing rights), net of related deferred tax liabilities ("adjusted" shareholders' equity or 
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: common shareholders' equity). Return on average tangible common shareholders' equity measures the Corporation's net income applicable to common shareholders as a percentage 
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: of adjusted average common shareholders' equity. The tangible common equity ratio represents adjusted ending common shareholders' equity divided by total tangible assets (total 
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: assets less goodwill and intangible assets (excluding mortgage servicing rights), net of related deferred tax liabilities). Return on average tangible shareholders' equity measures the 
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: Corporation's net income as a percentage of adjusted average total shareholders' equity. The tangible equity ratio represents adjusted ending shareholders' equity divided by total 
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: tangible assets. Tangible book value per common share represents adjusted ending common shareholders' equity divided by ending common shares outstanding. These measures are 
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: used to evaluate the Corporation's use of equity. In addition, profitability, relationship and investment models all use return on average tangible shareholders' equity as key measures 
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 3, Text: to support our overall growth goals.
Page: 34, Font Size: 7.0, Upper: False, Bold: False, block number: 4, Text: See the tables below for reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most closely related financial measures defined by GAAP for the six months ended June 30, 2023
